        <h1>Shock video sparks police hunt in Munich for migrant men who 'beat up two pensioners who tried to stop them from groping a woman on the subway'</h1>
<ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Video is said to have been recorded in the middle of the day on busy Metro</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Filmed moments after <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/germany/index.html">German </a>woman spurned asylum seeker's advances</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Claims to catch the moment 'Arab' men grapple with elderly commuters</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>One bald man can be seen held by the arms while another grabbed by neck</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Police have launched hunt for all people in the video for their investigation</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>See more news and stories from Germany at <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/germany/index.html">www.dailymail.co.uk/germany</a></strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Do you know these pensioners? Email immi.calderwood@mailonline.co.uk or call 0203 615 3230 </strong></font></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Imogen+Calderwood" class="author" rel="nofollow">Imogen Calderwood</a>


and 
<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Euan+McLelland" class="author" rel="nofollow">Euan McLelland</a>


and 
<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Flemming+Emil+Hansen+For+Mailonline" class="author" rel="nofollow">Flemming Emil Hansen For Mailonline</a>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">A shocking video of a group of migrant men attacking two pensioners who allegedly stopped them from groping a young woman on the subway  in Munich has sparked a police hunt. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">The footage shows the gang of around five men - who appear to be of 'Arab' origin - roughly seizing one elderly man by the arms as they shout abuse at him.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">The second elderly victim can be seen grappling with one of the gang, before he is held up by the neck and threatened.  </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Detectives in <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="" href="/news/germany/index.html">Germany </a>have today launched a hunt for the gang, and are appealing for witnesses to come forward in the criminal investigation. </font></p><div class="moduleFull mol-video"><a name="video" class="namedLink"></a><div class="item">
  <div class="vjs-video-container vjs-fixed vjs-span-two-col news" id="v-5358948752158442238">

</div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Munich man Tom Roth uploaded the footage - captured while travelling from Sendlinger Tor station to the Metro's city centre terminal - to his Facebook page.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">He said the fight broke out after a female passenger rejected the advances of one of the gang, after he placed his hand on her back. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">In response, the man smashed his hand against one of the carriage's glass windows - which caused outrage among the shocked passengers. </font></p><div><div class="related-carousel with-fb news half"
     id="p-15"
     data-track-module="am-related_carousel^related_carousel" data-track-selector=".rotator-panels a:not([class*=external])" data-track-pos="static">

</div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">When one of the elderly men asked the group to stop being so aggressive and leave the woman alone, one patted him mockingly on the head.   </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">That act of disrespect sparked a furious exchange.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">Translated, the post accompanying Mr Roth's video upload reads: 'A young woman  was attacked on the subway. When two old men tried to intervene, they too were attacked.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'This was in the heart of Munich, in the middle of the day. I got on the train at Sendlinger Tor travelling to the main railway station. I sat in a four-seater, across from a young lady.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'In the four-way behind her sat two asylum seekers. One of them, a young man, probably of Arab origin, bothered the woman.</font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-d807973a089509f8" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30C9B8B500000578-3426947-image-m-30_1454353570638.jpg" height="392" width="634" alt="Recorded on a mobile phone, the disgraceful video shows the men - of Eastern European or Arabic origin - holding one man by the arms as they verbally abuse him. The second victim is seen grappling with one of the migrants, before he is held up by the neck and threatened (pictured)" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">Recorded on a mobile phone, the disgraceful video shows the men - of Eastern European or Arabic origin - holding one man by the arms as they verbally abuse him. The second victim is seen grappling with one of the migrants, before he is held up by the neck and threatened (pictured)</p></div><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="splitLeft"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-9f0ecf57c61ae9b4" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30C9B8AC00000578-3426947-image-m-34_1454353615912.jpg" height="491" width="306" alt="" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div></div><div class="splitRight"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-ed255e8cb0d5e756" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30C9B8BD00000578-3426947-image-a-35_1454353628116.jpg" height="491" width="306" alt="Munich man Tom Roth uploaded the disgraceful video to his Facebook page. He caught the footage while travelling from Sendlinger Tor station to the Metro's city centre terminal" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div></div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">Munich man Tom Roth uploaded the disgraceful video to his Facebook page. He caught the footage while travelling from Sendlinger Tor station to the Metro's city centre terminal. He said the fight broke out after one of the asylum seekers was rejected by a woman who he had placed his hand upon on the train</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'He said something to her and asked: "Why will you not answer me in German?"</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'She responded: "Because you asked me in English". I think he had his hand on her back. She turned away and looked in my direction.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'As the train continued, the asylum seeker struck the glass window full force. I guess he was angry the woman rejected him. Several gentlemen shouted at him to stop.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'One of these men, in the four seats beside me, was then touched on the head by one of the asylum seekers wearing a brown jacket. He stroked his bald head, to mock him. It was such disrespectful behaviour, the likes of which I have rarely seen before.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'The gentleman  stood up right away. The asylum seeker then turned, approached the man and grabbed him by the neck. Everyone immediately became involved, with many trying to get in between the pair.</font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group"><div class="splitLeft"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-171e2f52c8c9fc80" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30C9B8C100000578-3426947-image-a-44_1454353698338.jpg" height="490" width="306" alt="Mr Roth claimed one asylum seeker smashed his hand against the carriage's glass window - an aggressive act of defiance the train's other passengers requested he desist" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div></div><div class="splitRight"><div class="mol-img">  <img id="i-ffde2a5290e0afde" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30C9B8C500000578-3426947-image-m-43_1454353695356.jpg" height="490" width="306" alt="When they did, one elderly German man was patted mockingly on the head by one of the migrant group. That act of disrespect sparked an angry exchange" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div></div><div class="clear"></div><p class="imageCaption">Mr Roth claimed one asylum seeker smashed his hand against the carriage's glass window - an aggressive act of defiance the train's other passengers requested he desist. When they did, one elderly German man was patted mockingly on the head by one of the migrant group. That act of disrespect sparked an angry exchange</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'The man's attacker  fell back in his four-seater. There were four asylum seekers now involved, staring at us and two other older gentlemen angrily.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'There were about 10-15 people beside and behind me. The situation was brought under control. When the train reached the station I shouted that I would call the police. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'Some of the other passengers yelled that they should leave the train, which they then did. I didn't call the police after all, since I have been told several times by friends that the police tell victims there's nothing they can do about it.'</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Police have today launched an investigation into the video, after finding it on 'a social network', which is reportedly focused on the man in the brown/orange jacket. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'We know about the video, after we found out about it on a social network,' a spokesman for Munich police department told MailOnline.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">‘Based on the video and the witness account we have decided to open a criminal investigation. We are in contact with a witness, but still need to identify the other people in the video.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">‘For starters, we need to find out whether any actual bodily harm and/or sexual harassment can be established.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">‘It would appear from the video that the aggressors have Arab backgrounds, but whether they are asylum seekers or not we can’t say at the moment.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">‘It’s mere speculation. We are working to identify them.’</font></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img" style="height: auto;">  <img id="i-5ff2534d7f79d467" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/2C430D9B00000578-3426947-The_incident_is_the_latest_violent_coming_together_of_asylum_see-a-58_1454354299020.jpg" height="405" width="634" alt="The incident is the latest violent coming together of asylum seekers and Germans to have come to light in recent weeks. Migrants are seen arriving by train at Munich Hauptbahnhof railway station on September 12 last year" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">The incident is the latest violent coming together of asylum seekers and Germans to have come to light in recent weeks. Migrants are seen arriving by train at Munich Hauptbahnhof railway station on September 12 last year</p></div><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img" style="height: auto;">  <img id="i-31fc4d02c5191c54" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/02/01/19/30BC034C00000578-3426947-It_follows_New_Year_riots_in_Cologne_triggered_by_a_number_of_se-a-57_1454354286844.jpg" height="404" width="634" alt="It follows New Year riots in Cologne triggered by a number of sexual assaults made against local women by a group of up to a 1,000 men 'of Arab and North African origin'" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">It follows New Year riots in Cologne triggered by a number of sexual assaults made against local women by a group of up to a 1,000 men 'of Arab and North African origin'</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">He added: ‘People should always call the police in such situations. We act straight away and will be there in a matter of minutes if something occurs in the subway. The public transportation in Munich is generally very safe.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">‘Things occur from time to time, but this is the first case of this sort I am aware of.’ </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">The incident is the latest violent coming together of asylum seekers and Germans to have come to light in recent weeks. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">It follows New Year riots in Cologne triggered by a number of sexual assaults made against local women by a group of up to a 1,000 men 'of Arab and North African origin'. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Police described the series of assaults against women outside the city's main train terminal as 'a completely new dimension of crime'.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Mr Roth stressed that after his own experience, he believes German chancellor Angela Merkel must now take action to protect the country's citizens.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">He said: 'I just felt the need to share this. Those involved were very distressed. An older lady said she doesn't leave her home at night any more. The two gentlemen said that it cannot go on like this.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">'I felt safer in Germany two or three years ago.  I find that terrifying and sad. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em">'I'm really sorry for the people who need help, but something must happen against the violent and disrespectful people among them. Many Asylum seekers have no respect for women, no respect for men - not even the old - let alone our laws and the police.' </font></p></div>

<script async src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 14.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
